)@@G@@*******     @[@@@@*.    @[@@@@*.    @F@@@@*.     THIS PROCEDURE PROCESSEYT
)@@G@@S THE THIRD FIELD OF THE BASE SGS'S @[@@@@*.    @G@@@@*.     IF THAT FIEYU
)@@G@@LD HAS THE NAME OF A GROUP OF ELEMENTS AS DEFINED     @[@@@@*.    @E@@@@YV
)@@G@@*.     BY THE GROUP SGS, THEN THE ELEMENTS IN THAT GROUP    @[@@@@*.    YW
)@@G@@@E@@@@*.     WILL BE PROCESSED IN THEIR TURN AS THOUGH TEMPORARY  @[@@@@YX
)@@G@@*.    @C@@@@*.     CORRECTIONS HAD BEEN ENTERED FOR THEM.   @[@@@@*.    YY
)@@G@@@#@@@@*DEFINE GROUPS    @C@@@@*SET MORE . WHEN THIS IS CLEAR, WE WILL EXYZ
)@@G@@IT    @C@@@@*SET I TO 0 . I WILL COUNT OUR POSITION IN TCF  @G@@@@*INCREZA
)@@G@@MENT KARD TO 2 WHILE MORE IS SET . SPECIAL KLUDGE TO LOOP FOREVER @C@@@@ZB

)@@G@@OUP [*K] [*J] . MAKE SURE THIS IS BASE    @B@@@@*IF FOUND IS SET . IT ISZK
)@@G@@ IN THE BASE SGS'S@A@@@@*PROCESS MAKETEMP GROUP [*K] [*J] . @E@@@@*ELSE ZL
)@@G@@. WE CAN'T MAKE CORRECTIONS IF WE DON'T KNOW THE ELT  @D@@@@#MSG,N ELT [ZM
)@@G@@GROUP,K,J,1] ON GROUP CARD [GROUP,K,1,1]  @A@@@@#MSG,N IS NOT ON A BASE ZN
)@@G@@SGS CARD.   @]@@@@#JUMP DONE  @[@@@@*END  @[@@@@*LOOP @ @@@@*ELSE . GROUZO
)@@G@@PID NOT DEFINED   @D@@@@*IF 1=+K . ONLY PRODUCE DIAGNOSTIC ON FIRST NO FZP
)@@G@@IND   @E@@@@#MSG,N [BASE,CARD,3,1] ON BASE CARD FOR ELT [BASE,CARD,1,1] ZQ
)@@G@@@B@@@@#MSG,N IS NOT ON ANY GROUP SGS DEFINITION.@]@@@@#JUMP DONE  @ @@@@ZR
)@@G@@*END . OF DIAGNOSTIC TEST     @B@@@@*SET K TO [GROUP] . FORCE EXIT FROM ZS

)@@G@@ ANOTHER BY THIS NAME   @[@@@@*END  @[@@@@*ELSE @G@@@@#MSG,N TCF ENTRY [ZU

)@@G@@@[@@@@*END  @D@@@@*SET MORE TO [TCF]-I . MORE SHOULD BE ZERO ON LAST ELTZW
